<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Autograph (assuming by Bach, which stylistic features suggest it is not, likewise BWV 576) has been lost. Source and sources (including the foregoing argument in detail) and structure discussed in Williams (Cambridge University Press, 2003), <i>The Organ Music of J. S. Bach</i>, pp.176â178.  
</p><p>Printings: Was in B&amp;H of course; was also in Band 9 of the Peters organ works edition - was this published earlier or later? (the first 7 volumes were certainly published earlier (by 1858) than the B&amp;H Complete, but I'm not sure about later volumes.) (ah. G&amp;R vol.9 - 1881).)- Schissel
</p>
